There are parks where you can soak your feet, parks that were transformed from quarries, and many new hotels. Although Yishang has been renovated, the interior of the room is still a bit old. The bedding is relatively comfortable, and it does not prevent the hot springs from being comfortable. In addition, guests can go in and out many times. The enthusiasm and initiative of the service staff also make up for some shortcomings. After checking in, they took the initiative to send us to the guest room. The originally arranged room had not been cleaned yet, and they took the initiative to change to other rooms. They were very meticulous.
Suggestions: I hope the catering content can be richer, and some aromatherapy can be put in the hot spring changing room. I feel that the smell of shoes and socks is a bit strong.
